Specifies the periodicity. \r\n    - Can be set to 'day', 'week', 'month' or 'year'. \r\n    - Defaults to 'day'\r\n- begin_date: \r\n    - Specifies the beginning date. \r\n    - Possible values: '2018', '2018-05', '2019-05-01', ..., ' 2017-03-02 05:34:19'\r\n    - Defaults to '1970-1-1 0:0:0'\r\n- end_date:\r\n    - Specifies the ending date.\r\n    - Possible values: '2018', '2018-05', '2019-05-01', ..., ' 2017-03-02 05:34:19'\r\n    - Defaults to the current date and time\r\n\r\n**Example Output:**\r\n`ag.code_changes('augur', period='year')`\r\n\r\n|         | commit_date           | count  |\r\n| ------------- |:-------------:| -----:|\r\n| 0      | 2017-01-01 00:00:00+00:00 |   1525 |\r\n| 1      | 2018-01-01 00:00:00+00:00  | 5140 |\r\n| 2 | 2019-01-01 00:00:00+00:00 |    711|\r\n\r\n`ag.code_changes('augur', period='month', begin_date='2018', end_date='2018-06')`\r\n\r\n|         | commit_date           | count  |\r\n| ------------- |:-------------:| -----:|\r\n|0 | 2018-01-01 00:00:00+00:00 |    99 |\r\n|1 | 2018-02-01 00:00:00+00:00 |    55 |\r\n|2 | 2018-03-01 00:00:00+00:00 |   105 |\r\n|3 | 2018-04-01 00:00:00+00:00 |   235 |\r\n|4 | 2018-05-01 00:00:00+00:00 |   506 |\r\n\r\n\r\nSigned-off-by: Parth Sharma <parth261297@gmail.com>	2019-05-28 18:44:41	2019-05-28 19:10:10	2019-05-28 19:10:10	2019-05-28 19:10:10	41591048390cecda6f77dd65d03707ca573b9af3	\N	\N	https://api.github.com/repos/chaoss/augur/pulls/284/commits	https://api.github.com/repos/chaoss/augur/pulls/284/comments	https://api.github.com/repos/chaoss/augur/pulls/comments{/number}	https://api.github.com/repos/chaoss/augur/issues/284/comments	https://api.github.com/repos/chaoss/augur/statuses/298d11a7d2bf77ad4b760d075c8624a5d7c75b2f	\N	\N	https://api.github.com/repos/chaoss/augur/issues/284	https://api.github.com/repos/chaoss/augur/issues/284/comments	https://api.github.com/repos/chaoss/augur/pulls/284/comments	https://api.github.com/repos/chaoss/augur/pulls/284/commits	https://api.github.com/repos/chaoss/augur/statuses/298d11a7d2bf77ad4b760d075c8624a5d7c75b2f	MEMBER	GitHub Pull Request Worker	0.0.1	GitHub API	2019-10-21 00:10:31	25430

(:issue:`1080`)\n> -   Restore the ``response`` argument to :exc:`~exceptions.Unauthorized`.\n>     (:pr:`1527`)\n> -   :exc:`~exceptions.Unauthorized` doesn't add the ``WWW-Authenticate``\n>     header if ``www_authenticate`` is not given. (:issue:`1516`)\n> -   The default URL converter correctly encodes bytes to string rather\n>     than representing them with ``b''``. (:issue:`1502`)\n> -   Fix the filename format string in\n>     :class:`~middleware.profiler.ProfilerMiddleware` to correctly handle\n>     float values. (:issue:`1511`)\n> -   Update :class:`~middleware.lint.LintMiddleware` to work on Python 3.\n>     (:issue:`1510`)\n> -   The debugger detects cycles in chained exceptions and does not time\n>     out in that case. (:issue:`1536`)\n> -   When running the development server in Docker, the debugger security\n>     pin is now unique per container.\n> \n> \n> Version 0.15.2\n> --------------\n> \n> Released 2019-04-02\n> \n> -   ``Rule`` code generation uses a filename that coverage will ignore.\n>     The previous value, "generated", was causing coverage to fail.\n>     (:issue:`1487`)\n> -   The test client removes the cookie header if there are no persisted\n>     cookies. This fixes an issue introduced in 0.15.0 where the cookies\n>     from the original request were used for redirects, causing functions\n>     such as logout to fail. (:issue:`1491`)\n> -   The test client copies the environ before passing it to the app, to\n>     prevent in-place modifications from affecting redirect requests.\n>     (:issue:`1498`)\n> -   The ``"werkzeug"`` logger only adds a handler if there is no handler\n>     configured for its level in the logging chain.
